## üìñ Quick Reference

### Test Structure Template

```typescript
test('FEATURE-AREA-001: should [expected behavior] when [condition]',
  { tag: '@spec' },
  async ({ page, startServerWithSchema }) => {
    // GIVEN: [initial context/setup]
    await startServerWithSchema({ ... })

    // WHEN: [action performed]
    await page.goto('/')

    // THEN: [expected outcome]
    await expect(page.locator(...)).toBeVisible()
  }
)
```

### Spec ID Format

| Prefix       | Area                     |
| ------------ | ------------------------ |
| `APP-`       | Application schema specs |
| `API-`       | API endpoint specs       |
| `STATIC-`    | Static generation specs  |
| `MIGRATION-` | Migration specs          |

### Commands

```bash
# Regenerate this file
bun run analyze:specs

# Run all specs
bun test:e2e:spec

# Run regression tests
bun test:e2e:regression

# Verify progress against GitHub
bun run analyze:specs --verify-progress
```
